***страшиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:страшиться.html>страши́ться</a> (11074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страшить.html>страши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strašítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страшиться.html>страши́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strašítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (+ genitive case)
</p>
<ol><li>to be afraid of, to dread, to fear</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страшить.html>страши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strašítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***страшно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:страшный.html>стра́шно</a> (987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страшный.html>стра́шный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strášnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страшный.html>стра́шно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strášno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-стра́шно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)страшне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-стра́шно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)страшне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>terrifyingly</li>
<li>very, badly</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>it is frightful, it is terrifying, one is scared
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:страшный.html>стра́шно</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>strášno</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm scared</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:страшный.html>стра́шный</a> (497)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>страх</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strax</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*straxъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*strākš-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)treg-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страшный.html>стра́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strášnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)страшне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)страшне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>terrible, scary <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional, in (e.g. one's rage)</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>ugly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ужасный.html>ужа́сный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">užásnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уродливый.html>уро́дливый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uródlivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***стращать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стращать.html>страща́ть</a> (22626)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стращать.html>страща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">straščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">застраща́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">постраща́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to frighten, to scare, to intimidate</li>
<li>to browbeat</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрекоза.html>стрекоза́</a> (15202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрекоза.html>стрекоза́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strekozá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрекоза.html>стрекозы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрекоза.html>стреко́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрекоза.html>стреко́з</a></b>)

***стрекотать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрекотать.html>стрекота́ть</a> (13901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, onomatopoeic. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">strīdeō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to squeak, to crack, to buzz, to whistle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">strīdō</i> (infinitive <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">strīdere</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τρίζω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trízō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to twitter, to squeak, to chirp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (perfect <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τέτρῑγα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tétrīga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στρίγξ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strínx</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(type of night bird)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (gen. sg. <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στρίγγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stríngos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрекотать.html>стрекота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strekotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to chirr <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of insects</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to rattle, to chatter <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of machine guns, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***стрела.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрела.html>стрела</a> (2649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*strěla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*strel-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*strēl-</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ster-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">line, streak, stripe; jet, spurt; beam</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрела.html>стрела́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strelá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрела.html>стрелы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрела.html>стре́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрела.html>стре́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>arrow</li>
<li>pointer, indicator</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shaft</li>
<li><i>(technical):</i> crane arm, jib, overhang beam, boom <i>(of a derrick)</i></li>
<li>derrick</li>
<li>cantilever</li>
<li>rise <i>(of an arch)</i>, camber</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стрелка</a> (23929)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрела.html>стрела́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strelá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стре́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strélka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стре́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стре́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стре́лок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hand, pointer, indicator</li>
<li>needle</li>
<li>railroad switch</li>
<li>arrow <i>(in a drawing)</i></li>
<li>promontory at a confluence of two rivers</li>
<li>crease <i>(of trousers)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">horses</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> frog</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> business meeting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забить.html>заби́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стре́лку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zabítʹ strélku</i> ― <small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">textile</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ladder</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стрело́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strelók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелковый.html>стрелко́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strelkóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rifle, infantry, shooting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелковый.html>стрелко́вое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оружие.html>ору́жие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>strelkóvoje</b> orúžije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">small arms</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелковый.html>стрелко́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:полк.html>полк</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>strelkóvyj</b> polk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">infantry/rifle regiment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелковый.html>стрелко́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кружок.html>кружо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>strelkóvyj</b> kružók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shooting circle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелковый.html>стрелко́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спорт.html>спорт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>strelkóvyj</b> sport</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shooting</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***стрельнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрельнуть.html>стрельну́ть</a> (15463)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелять.html>стреля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">streljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрельнуть.html>стрельну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strelʹnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелять.html>стреля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shoot <i>(at)</i>, to fire <i>(at)</i>, to fire a shot <i>(at)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cadge, to scrounge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стрельнуть.html>стрельну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигарета.html>сигаре́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>strelʹnútʹ</b> sigarétu u kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sponge/scrounge a cigarette from smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрелять.html>стреля́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигарета.html>сигаре́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on vsegdá streljájet u menjá sigaréty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to he's always cadging cigarettes from/off me</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***стрелять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрелять.html>стреля́ть</a> (926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стрѣляти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strěljati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">throw arrows</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелять.html>стреля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">streljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстрелить.html>вы́стрелить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрельнуть.html>стрельну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shoot, to fire
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелять.html>стреля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушка.html>пу́шек</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воробей.html>воробья́м</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>streljátʹ</b> iz púšek po vorobʹjám</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to use a sledgehammer to crack a nut, to break a butterfly on the wheel, to crush a fly with a steam-roller</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">to shoot from cannons at sparrows</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shoot <i>feel acute pains</i></li>
<li>to cadge</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелять.html>стреля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">streljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стреляться.html>стреля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">streljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li>to fight a duel <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to commit suicide

<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́стрелиться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výstrelitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стрельну́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">strelʹnútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***стремглав.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стремглав.html>стремгла́в</a> (18565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">стрьмоглавъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strĭmoglavŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with the head down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> via Russian Church Slavonic forms стрьмъглавъ, стремоглавъ, стремглавъ, which acquired modern meaning in 15th century, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*strьmъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golva</i> + <span class="Latinx" lang="sla-pro">*-ь</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стремглав.html>стремгла́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stremgláv</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>precipitately, very fast, headlong
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Иван Сергеевич Тургенев (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ivan_Turgenev" class="extiw" title="w:Ivan Turgenev">Ivan Sergeyevich Turgenev</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a></cite>  | <cite>The Watch</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>Но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устоять.html>устоя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:надел.html>наде́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:броситься.html>бро́сился</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стремглав.html>стремгла́в</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:показывать.html>пока́зывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рок</a> Давыду.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">No ja uže ne mog ustojátʹ na méste, nadél na sebjá časý i brósilsja <b>stremgláv</b> pokázyvatʹ svoj podárok Davydu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">But I could not stand still, I put on my watch and rushed <b>headlong</b> to show my gift to David.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> with the head down, headlong
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Leo Tostoy, <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Митенька <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стремглав.html>стремгла́в</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слететь.html>слете́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ступень.html>ступе́ней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:убежать.html>убежа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:клумба.html>клу́мбу</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mitenʹka <b>stremglav</b> sletel s šesti stupenej i ubežal v klumbu.</i></dd><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***стремительный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стремительный.html>стреми́тельный</a> (5420)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стреми́ть(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stremítʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стремительный.html>стреми́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stremítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>impetuous, violent, rash, headlong</li>
<li>rapid, swift</li></ol>

***стремиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стремиться.html>стреми́ться</a> (1702)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стреми́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stremítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стремиться.html>стреми́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stremítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устремиться.html>устреми́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to aspire, to strive, to aim, to long, to crave
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стремиться.html>стреми́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:юг.html>юг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stremítʹsja</b> na jug</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to long to go south</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стремиться.html>стреми́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́де</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stremítʹsja</b> k svobóde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to yearn to be free</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tend (to/toward)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i>x</i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стремиться.html>стреми́тся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бесконечность.html>бесконе́чности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i>x</i> <b>stremítsja</b> k beskonéčnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><i>x</i> <b>is tending</b> toward infinity</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to speed, to rush</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стреми́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stremítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***стремя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стремя.html>стре́мя</a> (14821)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stremę</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*strьmę</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">strzemię</i>, etc.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стремя.html>стре́мя</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strémja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стремя.html>стре́мени</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стремя.html>стремена́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стремя.html>стремя́н</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стременно́й</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стремя́нный</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стре́мечко</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stirrup</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stapes</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
